Responding to the Heated European Situation: Italy and Germany Cooperate Vigorously, Hoping to Facilitate a Western European Security Pact, Supporting the New Government of the Spanish Revolution, The Two Countries Stand on a Common Front Against Russia, The Italian Foreign Minister Issues a Statement on the Verge of Departing Berlin 42

Munich – Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano, after visiting Germany and holding talks with Führer Hitler and Foreign Minister Neurath, and after completing his mission, flew back to Rome from here at 10:15 this morning. (Havas, 25th)

(Berlin) Before his departure, Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano made a statement to visiting reporters, outlining the progress made by Italy and Germany in recent discussions on important European issues as follows:

(1) Italy and Germany have jointly responded to the notes from Britain, expressing their willingness to cooperate in concluding a security pact in Asia and Europe.

(2) Italy and Germany have decided to maintain close and friendly contact on the issue of the League of Nations.

(3) Italy and Germany have further decided to cooperate closely to deal with the Danube River issue. At the same time, both countries expressed great satisfaction with the practical and beneficial results obtained by Austria.

(4) Italy and Germany have agreed to support the government led by General Franco in the Spanish Civil War, as it is capable of restoring order within Spain. However, they will continue to adhere to the principle of non-intervention and maintain all international obligations.

(5) Regarding the threat of Bolshevism, Italy and Germany have decided to concentrate their efforts to safeguard the sacred qualities of European civilization. An agreement on the exchange of culture between Germany and Italy will be drafted soon.

(6) Business activities of Italy and Germany in Abyssinia have been considerably adjusted. All difficulties will be addressed jointly to eliminate them. (Reuters, 25th)

(Rome) An article in the Italian newspaper, mouthpiece of the government, written by Mr. Gayda, states that an agreement between Germany and Italy on major European issues will be announced today. Germany's recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia is a prelude to the agreement. The agreement will involve the Locarno Pact, the reconstruction of Europe, the League of Nations, Spain, the Danube region, economic relations, communism, and other matters. It is widely believed that Germany and Italy will also establish another agreement in which Italy agrees to support Germany's demand to recover its colonies; however, this agreement may not be announced today. (Reuters, 25th)

Munich – Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano held talks with Führer Hitler this morning in the nearby city of Berchtesgaden for two hours. As news reporters were not allowed to enter the Führer's villa, the details of the meeting are unknown. After the talks, Hitler hosted a banquet for Ciano, attended by 25 people, including German Foreign Minister Neurath, the newly appointed Ambassador to Britain Ribbentrop, Ambassador to Italy Hassell, and Italian Ambassador to Germany Attolico. After the banquet, Ciano took his leave, and the Führer personally escorted him to the door. (Havas, 24th)

(Reuters, 24th) The French Radical Party Resolves to Maintain the People's Front, Six Political Principles, Urging the Government to Implement Them

French Radical Party Resolves to Maintain the People's Front, Six Political Principles, Urging the Government to Implement Them 44

Biarritz, France – The congress of the Radical Socialist Party concluded this afternoon at 8:00 PM. The resolution proposed by the party leader, Minister of National Defense Daladier, was unanimously passed. The resolution was a compromise of proposals from various factions and was drafted with the consent of the Speaker of the Chamber of Deputies, Herriot, Minister without Portfolio Zay, and former Prime Minister Sarraut. The resolution asserted that the Radical Socialist Party should continue to support the People's Front cabinet while not abandoning the party's main political principles. The resolution began by quoting the famous "Declaration of the Rights of Man" promulgated during the French Revolution, stating that the "Declaration of the Rights of Man" is the fundamental law of democracy, which stipulates that private property shall not be infringed. Occupying factories, farms, and shops harms the freedom of the people and cannot be tolerated. The resolution then listed the various political principles of the Radical Party, stating that they must be fully adopted. These political principles are as follows:

(1) Safeguarding international peace and respecting the constraints stipulated in the Covenant of the League of Nations; (2) Strengthening national defense; (3) Maintaining domestic order, abiding by the rule of law, dissolving and disarming all illegal organizations; (4) Resolving social disputes through mediation and compulsory arbitration; (5) Maintaining national authority and not allowing it to be undermined in any way, especially not allowing it to be manipulated and utilized by large corporations; (6) Striving to balance the budget.

The final paragraph of the resolution stated, "The Radical Socialist Party Congress hereby expresses its trust in the representatives of this party participating in the current government and requests them to continue to safeguard the implementation of the various political principles of the Radical Party within the scope of the government's actions." Before the opening of this Radical Socialist Party Congress, there was widespread fear that the party might withdraw from the People's Front due to the activities of the Communist Party and social unrest. Now that the above resolution has been unanimously passed by the congress, indicating continued participation in the People's Front and support for the current government, the French political situation will be clarified, like seeing a blue sky after clearing away the clouds.

Heated Debate During Political Discussions 45

Biarritz – The Radical Socialist Party Congress continued its session this afternoon, discussing general political issues. After intense debate, the draft resolution of the party leader Daladier was unanimously passed (see separate dispatch). When the congress convened this afternoon, Minister without Portfolio Zay gave a speech, requesting that the representatives attending the congress use moderate language when expressing their opinions to avoid triggering a terrible political tide. Zay said that Prime Minister Blum must strive to maintain a balance between the left and right factions within the People's Front and that his task was extremely difficult and should be forgiven. Then, Mr. Campinchi, the chairman of the Radical Socialist Party's parliamentary group and the rapporteur on general political issues, gave a speech, acknowledging that the current political unrest was caused by social turmoil, and therefore, the occupation of factories by workers must be opposed, lest foreigners think that France has become Bolshevik. Regarding the Communist Party, he said that the Communist Party's policy changes were too sudden, and its proclaimed patriotism was also too exaggerated. However, since the Paris riots of February 6, 1934, the Communist Party has consistently expressed its determination to safeguard the republican system, which the Radical Socialist Party cannot forget. Next, Mr. Roche, the leader of the Northern Department branch, stated that it was a great mistake for the Radical Party to join the People's Front hand in hand with the Communist Party because the Communist Party regarded the People's Front as a prelude to the establishment of a Soviet system. Although the Communist Party swore to fight for peace and bread, it actually held meetings every day to agitate and restrain the government's actions, which could be said to be breaking its promises. Next, Mr. Kessel, a member of parliament of the Radical Socialist Party, gave a speech, saying, "This party should now declare that it will no longer tolerate the occupation of factories by workers. However, we should also guarantee the labor class that the new social laws promulgated by the government must be implemented uniformly, and even the most stubborn employers must abide by them." Regarding the Communist Party, he said that the Radical Party would never break with any group in the People's Front and that the People's Front must unite to jointly defend the republic and the motherland. Next, Mr. Banat, a member of the Radical Socialist Party, stated that once the People's Front collapsed, people like Laval and Doumergue (both former prime ministers) would inevitably stage a comeback, and the harm would be unimaginable. Now, in order to preserve the internal unity of the People's Front, both employers and employees must abide by order. Next, former Minister of the Interior Marchandeau stated that members of the Radical Party should not forget their original political principles and should not allow outsiders to doubt the true radicalism. Fascism and communism both deceive the people, and their dangers are the same. We must not be blinded by them. Next, former Minister of Education Gno stated that the Radical Socialist Party should continue to participate in the People's Front government because there would be no way to produce a majority in parliament without the cooperation of the Socialist Party. Moreover, the current government has completed various reforms thoroughly and quickly, so that the people and the parliament can be harmonious. Finally, Minister of National Defense Daladier gave a speech, refuting Roche's attack on the Communist Party, saying, "Today, the whole of Europe is competing in new mysticism, but we are not. We have nothing mystical to say. We French people have our own social ideals and are not a rabble." At this point, Daladier read out the draft resolution, which was unanimously passed by the congress. (Havas, 24th)

Prime Minister Blum Reiterates His Beliefs 46

Toulouse – Prime Minister Blum delivered a long speech at the theater here today, reiterating his belief in the People's Front government, saying that he would certainly be able to show something in the government's various undertakings in the future. He also said, "The most profound meaning of the current political experience lies in determining whether the coalition government of republican democracy and labor class democracy can act effectively without deviating from the methods of democracy and damaging the principles of freedom. I believe that we will be able to present concrete evidence to the world to reach a consensus, that is, the various social laws passed by our parliament are based on the freedom of organization of the labor class and the joint cooperation of all those who participate in creating the country." Blum continued, "If a socialist system can be established throughout the world, then war will not only be impossible but will also become inconceivable. Can democracy and democracy guarantee peace, or will they inevitably be subjugated by individual power? This is a difficult test being conducted in France, Europe, and even the world." Blum concluded his speech by saying, "We are striving to expand the negotiations among the signatory countries of the Locarno Pact in order to solve general European problems. In short, our political program is nothing else but trusting the diligent France and the peaceful Europe." (Havas, 24th)

No Fear of Shortage of War Materials, Morale of Spanish Government Troops is High, Pozas Appointed Commander-in-Chief of the Central Route, Fierce Fighting on the Southwestern Front of the Capital 48

Madrid – Political circles here expressed great satisfaction with the Soviet Union's decision to effectively withdraw from the non-intervention agreement in the Spanish Civil War, hoping that they would be able to purchase military supplies from the Soviet Union in the future, which would quickly change the war situation and benefit the government. The panic in the capital cannot be concealed, but since former Minister of the Interior General Pozas was appointed commander-in-chief of the government army, the residents have become more optimistic. Pozas served as the director of the security forces in the early stages of the rebellion and showed his wisdom in protecting the capital. The government militia has now been properly organized in accordance with military law, so it is no longer as undisciplined as before. The difficulties of lacking war materials are expected to be eliminated. At the same time, General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the National Army, has ordered his troops to temporarily stop attacking the capital so that the soldiers can rest. However, its air force is still very active, bombing the government troops' positions every day with the aim of destroying the morale of the defending troops and destroying the government troops' trenches. The National Army claims to have broken through the second line of defense of the government troops in Mostoles, twelve miles from the capital. (Reuters, 25th)

Madrid – The government is now actively reorganizing the supreme command and appointing former Minister of the Interior Pozas as commander-in-chief of the central front. Pozas told reporters from this agency that the morale of the government troops is now very high. Currently, the fiercest fighting is in the area of Illescas (more than 30 kilometers southwest of the capital), that is, between the city and the road from Madrid to Aranjuez. The rebel army is now attacking the area from the north, using artillery to bombard on land and airplanes to bomb from the air. Therefore, the government troops had to withdraw from the towns of Borox and Cesiña. When the rebel planes attacked, the reporter from this agency was on the scene and suffered a slight injury to the neck. The government troops fought bravely regardless of their lives, and their loyalty is admirable. (Havas, 24th)

Burgos – Special dispatch from the reporter of this agency: The National Army is now taking the offensive on two main fronts, one is in the direction of Madrid, and the other is advancing from the city of Oviedo in the northwest towards the city of Gijón. The entire line in the direction of Madrid is fifty kilometers wide, and in some places, especially in the area of Navalcarnero southwest of the capital, it has reached 35 kilometers from the city of Madrid. In addition, the city of El Escorial northwest of the capital can be captured at any moment, but the government troops are trying to open a road in front of the city. As for the area of Oviedo, the National Army has defeated the government troops and is pursuing them towards the port of Gijón and the city of Trobia. (Havas, 25th)

People are Panic-Stricken, the Capital is Defending Against Air Raids 49

Madrid – The Spanish capital is prepared for enemy air raids today. Residents are looking up at the sky, so that all normal activities have completely stopped. The number of vehicles and pedestrians on the road has been greatly reduced. However, there are still male and female orators shouting loudly in the streets and alleys, striving for resistance in order to win. Now that the rebel army has intensified its encirclement, the capital's food is also in danger. However, the government leaders have no intention of surrendering and know that after the rebel army wins, all trade unions will not be able to exist. Therefore, they have ordered trade union members between the ages of 18 and 40 to abandon their jobs and join the army. (National Telegram, 24th)

Railway Transportation is Cut Off 50

Madrid – Special dispatch from the reporter of this agency accompanying the army on the front line in Illescas, south of the capital: After the government troops and the National Army clashed today on the road from Toledo to Madrid and the Tagus River, railway transportation between Madrid and the east has been cut off. From now on, Madrid can only communicate with the southeastern coastal city of Valencia via highway. It is said that three columns of the National Army are now advancing forward. One team is advancing north by ten kilometers and will cut off the road from the capital to Toledo. The other two columns are advancing east by fifteen kilometers and will cut off the railway from the capital to Cuenca. (Havas, 24th)

Militia Surround Oviedo 51

Madrid – The government has just issued a bulletin stating that the militia composed of miners in Asturias Province in the northwest has now surrounded the city of Oviedo and successively occupied the three towns of Cairo, San Lazaro, and Xinmatinalia in the suburbs. As for the National Army in Toledo south of the capital and Aragon Province in the northeast, it was also repelled by the government troops. The infantry units belonging to the government army also advanced three kilometers in the south towards the city of Villabrang. However, according to a broadcast message issued by the National Army's radio station in La Coruña, the National Army is continuing to advance towards Madrid. After a fierce battle with the government troops, it has occupied the three villages of Cesena, Esquivias, and Borox. In this battle, more than 300 government troops were killed, many artillery pieces and machine guns were captured, and countless prisoners were taken, including many young girls. According to a broadcast message issued by the National Army's radio station in Seville, 40 National Army bombers and 42 fighter planes scattered leaflets over Madrid yesterday morning, warning residents to surrender immediately. By the afternoon, 160 more planes appeared in the sky to scatter leaflets. The National Army's radio station in La Coruña also issued a message confirming this incident, saying that the residents of the capital were greatly panicked when they saw a large number of planes circling in the sky, and many people were hit by bullets and injured. Yesterday, about 300 women held a demonstration in front of the Ministry of the Interior, demanding that the government surrender to the National Army, and they were dispersed by the police. (Havas, 25th)

Widely Rumored in London that the Soviet Union is Shipping Military Supplies to Spain, the Non-Intervention Coordination has Broken Down, the International Situation is Tense 52

(London) According to a message received here from the port of Istanbul, Turkey, a Soviet cargo ship passed through the Dardanelles Strait this morning and entered the Mediterranean Sea. The ship was carrying a large number of military armaments, especially many artillery pieces placed on the deck, which could be clearly seen. The newspapers also carried reports tonight that 30 Soviet cargo ships are now in the Mediterranean Sea, heading towards the port of Barcelona in Spain. Diplomatic circles here are very uneasy after hearing the news, believing that the Soviet Union had said that it would reserve the right to supply the Spanish government troops with military armaments depending on the situation of other countries providing assistance to the Spanish rebel army. What it said may have been put into practice. If so, it may cause serious incidents. According to news from Berlin, as a result of the talks between Italy and Germany, it has been decided to adopt a common attitude towards the internal turmoil in Spain and actively prevent other countries from providing assistance to the Spanish government troops. According to this, when Soviet cargo ships sail into Spanish ports, they may be intercepted by warships of certain countries, which is also unknown. The tense situation will then tend to be extreme. Political circles here commented on the Portuguese government's severance of diplomatic relations with the Spanish government, saying that Portugal now believes that Madrid is about to fall. At that time, the country will recognize the Spanish National Army government and dispatch formal envoys. As for Britain, it does not intend to regard the National Army government as a formal government, but only recognizes it as one of the belligerent groups. This is the same as when the Italian army captured the capital of Abyssinia, Britain recognized the commander-in-chief of the Italian army as the same example. (Havas, 24th)

Britain also Sent a Letter to the Adjustment Committee, Accusing Russia of Violating the Agreement 53

(London) The British government sent a letter to the Non-Intervention Adjustment Committee in the Spanish Civil War, which accused Russia of three violations of the non-intervention agreement and Italy of one violation. The letter was transmitted to the members of the committee late yesterday. The accusations against Russia were: (1) On October 18, the Russian ship "Stachei Bolshevik" arrived at the fortified port of Cartagena, 326 miles southeast of Madrid, and unloaded a total of 18 disassembled aircraft, 15 tanks, and more than 300 boxes of bombs and other military supplies; (2) About two weeks ago, the Spanish ship "Combes" also unloaded several artillery pieces and mortars made by the Soviet Union, as well as rifles and other military supplies, at the port of Cartagena; (3) On October 19, the Russian ship "Qiuxuqifu" unloaded 85 Russian-made military trucks and Russian-made tires at the port of Alicante. The accusation against Italy was that on October 1, three Italian planes flew down to the port of Palma in the Balearic Islands. Around that day, an Italian ship unloaded several boxes of military equipment and bullets in the port.

Asking Russia to Continue to Clarify Whether it is Still Bound by the Agreement 54

At the same time, Mr. Maisky, the Russian Ambassador to Britain, under the strong pressure of other members of the Non-Intervention Committee, has applied for the Soviet government to continue to clarify the letter that the country submitted on Friday, declaring its effective withdrawal from the committee's non-intervention agreement. It is heard that the committee has raised a special issue and wishes the Soviet Union to answer it clearly, that is, "Whether the Soviet Union will continue to regard itself as bound by the same conditions of the agreement as other participating countries in the agreement." Lord Plymouth, the chairman of the committee, declared yesterday at the meeting of the subcommittee that he did not understand the meaning of the letter presented by the Soviet Union. The Italian Ambassador to Britain, Mr. Grandi, then rose to speak, saying that the Soviet Union had determined that other countries had violated the non-intervention agreement without waiting for the committee to decide everything in accordance with the meeting procedures. Mr. Grandi refused to discuss the points in Russia's accusation against Italy, saying that he should first understand whether Mr. Maisky's presence still represented a government bound by the agreement, or was merely an observer. If Russia was only an observer, it would not be appropriate to allow it to attend the meeting. Thereupon, the German Chargé d'Affaires in Britain, Mr. Bismarck, and the French Ambassador to Britain, Mr. Corbin, both urged for clarification of the Russian letter. When the subcommittee began to consider increasing the strength of the non-intervention agreement, Mr. Maisky again proposed the Soviet Union's proposal to control Portuguese ports by the British and French naval fleets, but the meeting expressed the opinion that the Soviet Union's proposal was difficult to implement. Lord Plymouth informally proposed sending a delegation to various ports in Spain to investigate everything, but the public did not make a decision on this point.

Under Strict Security in Beijing: Left and Right Wing Demonstrations; Both Sides Shout Slogans Without Conflict; Leader of the Rexist Party Arrested 55

Brussels: Today was the day the fascist Rexist Party held a demonstration. Brussels: Although the fascist Rexist Party was scheduled to hold a demonstration today, the general impression in Beijing last night was that tensions had eased. It seems that Rexist Party leader Degrelle's plan to gather party members and enter Beijing has been abandoned. Grain Prices Soar Uncontrollably in Northern Anhui, Breaking All Previous Records; Authorities Seek to Stabilize Market Prices 60

Bengbu Correspondence: In northern Anhui, after years of floods and droughts, the rural economy has declined drastically, and low grain prices have hurt farmers, creating a widespread phenomenon. Unexpectedly, in recent months, grain prices have soared step by step, which is the opposite of the situation in previous years. Most of the poor farmers have suffered greatly. The grain markets in various counties do not reduce the soaring high prices due to the autumn harvest. Taking Bengbu city as an example, the recent market price of wheat has risen to $18.40 per stone, soybeans to $14.40 per stone, sesame to $19.50 per stone, rice to $18.80 per stone, sorghum to $10.40 per stone. The supply of miscellaneous grains is scarce, and the price has skyrocketed, breaking all previous records and reaching the peak. The reasons for this are nothing more than three: 1. There has been no rain for more than a month, and the weather is very dry, making it difficult to sow winter wheat. Droughts have become a disaster in various counties, and farmers are worried that there will be a famine year, so they hoard new grains and are reluctant to sell them quickly. The market is short of grain, leading to a situation where supply cannot meet demand. 2. The situation is uncertain and the people are frightened. The farmers in northern Anhui have little knowledge and do not understand the circulating legal tender at all. They are suspicious and worry that it would be better to hoard grain than to sell it, regardless of market demand. 3. In North China, people from a certain country secretly instructed unscrupulous merchants to purchase huge amounts of grain and transport it for export. Unscrupulous merchants only care about profits and disregard the people's food, so they try their best to manipulate the market. The grain in Jiangsu and Anhui is also being absorbed. Due to these three reasons, grain prices in northern Anhui have reached the highest record. The price of flour, which is needed by the citizens for daily use, has also increased with the price of grain, rising from $3.20 per bag to $4.10 per bag. Amid the people's worries, there is still a tendency for prices to rise. The local authorities here believe that if grain prices continue to soar, the people's food will be at risk. Recently, they invited officials and gentry to a meeting at the Public Security Bureau to discuss ways to stabilize grain prices. It was resolved that the two chiefs of the Water and Land Public Security Bureaus, Lu and Jiang, would contact the persons in charge of the two flour mills, Xinfengbao and Yu, to restrict the price of flour from rising again while the price of wheat has not risen. As for stabilizing grain prices, the Chamber of Commerce will convene all industries to discuss relief measures to maintain the people's food. (24th)

Negotiations on Municipal Debt with Japanese Nationals in Xiamen; Japanese Consul First Proposed $370,000; Audited Amount is Over $260,000; Second Proposal Mostly Has No Record 61

Xiamen Correspondence: Since the reconstruction of the urban area in Xiamen in 1925, opening up roads, filling land, and building dikes, the work was mainly handled by the Municipal Council, the Road Administration Office, and the Dike Construction Office. During this period, private land and houses were acquired at estimated values. The work concluded in 1934. At that time, due to the drastic drop in land prices, no one bid on the official land, and some of the debts remained unpaid, some of which were owed to foreign nationals, with the majority being Japanese. On May 17 of this year, the Japanese Consulate in Xiamen sent a letter to the municipal government, proposing an unpaid debt of more than 270,000 yuan for the acquisition of houses and land belonging to Japanese nationals by the former Road Administration Office, requesting payment. The municipal government believed that this debt was not limited to foreign nationals, and that many Chinese people were also owed money, so it decided to reorganize the entire situation. The Road Administration Debt Reorganization Committee was jointly formed by the municipal government and various sectors in July to begin the reorganization. The debt proposed by the Japanese consul was also submitted for review. Unexpectedly, on the 13th of this month, the Japanese consul sent another letter to the municipal government, for the second time proposing the unresolved debts of Japanese nationals, stating that "Regarding the 21 Japanese nationals, including Li Yongfu, who were owed more than 370,000 silver dollars by the former Road Administration Office, this consulate sent a letter on May 17 of this year for your reference and action. It is now heard that your government has organized a Debt Reorganization Committee and has concrete measures for repaying old debts. However, there are still many lands and houses owned by Japanese nationals that were acquired or demolished by the Chinese authorities at that time that have not yet been resolved. A list is enclosed for your reference, and it is planned to send personnel to negotiate and gradually resolve the matter." The total amount listed was 987,400 yuan. After the municipal government handed over the debt list to the Bureau of Public Works, item-by-item verification and signing was carried out, revealing that most of it had no record to check, and the remaining parts were improperly authorized or not recognized by the Chinese side according to law. The bureau sent it to the Debt Reorganization Committee for review. The committee held a regular meeting on the 20th and clearly verified the debt proposed by the Japanese consul for the first time. The number of debts owed to Japanese nationals was calculated as follows: purchase fees for which payment vouchers had been issued but not paid were 71,002 yuan, 9 jiao, 8 fen, 9 li; purchase fees for which contracts had not been paid and payment vouchers had not been issued were 15,647 yuan, 3 jiao, 5 fen; loans and refunds of land prices were 173,987 yuan, 2 jiao, 4 fen, totaling 260,637 yuan, 5 jiao, 7 fen, 9 li. In addition, 31,515 yuan, 4 jiao, 4 fen, could not be listed as debt. The interest on the above-listed loans and refunds of land prices will not be listed for the time being and will be discussed again during the debt settlement. Detailed lists are available for all of the above items. This is the debt proposed by the Japanese consul for the first time that has been verified, recorded, and recognized for settlement. Regarding the 987,400 yuan proposed for the second time, the Debt Reorganization Committee decided that "The list of unresolved debts of Japanese nationals sent by the Japanese consul will be submitted to the Municipal Government through the Bureau of Public Works after detailed review. It is still under review. Most of the debts proposed by the Japanese consul for the second time involve official properties and public lands that Japanese nationals claim to own. At that time, the Road Administration Office ordered them to submit property deeds, but they could not submit them, so their ownership was revoked. A portion of the debt involved compensation for the loss of cemeteries ceded for roads. There are also beaches that have been filled into embankments by the Dike Construction Office, but Japanese nationals claim to own the property and demand compensation for the land price. The Japanese side does not dare to claim that all of the debts registered for the second time are based on factual evidence, so they requested that personnel be sent to consult with the Debt Reorganization Committee to verify and resolve each item. The future resolution of this "no record to check" debt will require considerable negotiation. (October 23)

Recent Conditions in Guangdong and Guangxi (10): The Distinguished Guests of the Lequn Society 62

— By Our Reporter Xiao'an

The establishment of the Lequn Society is mainly for Party, military, and government agencies, and is used to entertain guests. In recent years, Guangxi has been working hard on construction, and many people have come from afar to Guangxi to visit. At the same time, the Guangxi authorities have also hired scholars and experts from all fields to give lectures or guide the direction of construction. The Party, military, and government authorities have all entertained those who came to Guizhou. If they were to live in various hotels, it would be inconvenient. Therefore, the Lequn Society was organized, and the society was responsible for entertaining guests. Therefore, the interior of the society is quiet and similar to a YMCA, and it is also landscaped. It is said that the site of the society was once the private residence of Lu Rongting. After Lu's defeat, it became public property. Today, Lu's son, Yu Guang, still lives across the street from the society. The scope of the society is very large. Entering the gate is a garden, and cars can directly enter the garden. The western-style building in the center is the Lequn Hall. The reception and lodging departments are on the upper floor. The red railing at the top of the building, illuminated by electric lights at night, is vaguely visible under the green willows and white poplars, making it extremely elegant and lovely. Downstairs, there is a library, billiards room, western restaurant, and Chinese restaurant. Behind the Lequn Hall is a square, with lush green bamboo that is taller than the eaves. Every morning and evening, one can watch the fallen leaves flutter, and the feeling is distant and peaceful. The rear seat is a three-story western-style building, named Youth Building, which is divided into the office of the Director-General, a conference hall, a board of directors room, an entertainment department, a cultural department, a chess room, a gymnasium, and a friendship hall. To the left of Lequn Hall and the Youth Building is Le Yuan. There is a lake in the garden, with a lake center pavilion in the middle. There are nine-turn bridges in the front and back that can be used to pass through. The four weeks of the garden are planted with exotic flowers and herbs. Outside the lake, there is a green lawn, a music pavilion, and a tennis court. The area of the court is quite large, and the layout is very complete. It is much better to use this as a place to entertain guests than ordinary hotels, and guards are placed in front of the door. High-ranking officials often come to the society to play and feast with guests, which is especially safe. Therefore, the people of Guizhou call it a guesthouse, not a hostel. There are twenty-four rooms in the society. The cheapest room rent is one dollar per day, and the most expensive is twelve dollars. However, there are those who are discussed on a weekly basis and those who are discussed on a monthly basis. Members are calculated at a 20% discount. Therefore, even if they are not people who are entertained by the Party, military, and government authorities, they can also live in the society. The society is open at any time to accept tourists who travel to Nanning, unless it is during a period when it is ordered to entertain guests.

When the reporter arrived in Nanning, it happened to be the beginning of the Fourth Army Group Headquarters' order to carry out demobilization. The Headquarters had just summoned the military and division commanders of each army, as well as the commanders of the militia regiments, to discuss the demobilization plan and training plan. The person in charge of the society initially told me that it was full, which shows the grandeur of the situation. Later, the person in charge inquired with the hostel department and learned that Qu Shounian had returned to Yonglin earlier in the morning, so they used the room where Qu had lived to accommodate the reporter. At that time, the people who were living in the society also included Central Committee Member Liu Luyin and Mr. Wang Zhisheng. In the course of our idle conversation, I learned that Liu Luyin had gone to Liuzhou and Guilin for sightseeing and had not returned. Anhui Province Drought Panic: Grain Prices Soar, Plague Rampant, Inland River Launches Suspend Navigation 63

Wuhu Dispatch: Anhui Province originally relied heavily on agricultural products. This year, after the autumn harvest, for nearly two months, the sky has been clear for thousands of miles, with no rain. The fields are scorched, and everything is withered. It's difficult for wheat seeds to enter the soil, and the growth of beans and vegetables is difficult. Drought conditions have already appeared in various places, and the serious signs of spring famine have greatly threatened the entire population. The soaring grain prices are an abnormal phenomenon that hasn't been seen in many years. Although foreign merchants are actively purchasing, the sources are scarce. The fact that the prolonged drought will cause a spring famine has a greater impact. Various firms, including Yanjin and Guangdong-Chaozhou, have been vying to purchase grain in Wuhu in recent days, especially the Yanjin firms, which have spread rumors about the puppet Manchukuo purchasing and hoarding grain, which has further caused panic about food. In Lujiang, which produces the most rice, ordinary indica rice has surged to eight yuan and three jiao per shi. Superior quality rice also sells for eight yuan, one jiao, and two fen. Superior quality machine-milled rice in Nanling has even reached eight yuan, seven jiao, and eight fen. Other counties, such as Chaoxian, Qingyang, Wuwei, and Tongcheng, have also reached more than eight yuan. The market prices of miscellaneous grains such as wheat, beans, and sesame have all exceeded the records of recent years. Every day, as much as 10,000 to 20,000 bags of rice are gathered in Wuhu for export. Therefore, the rising prices are unknown. The rising prices are unknown and the extent is also unknown. Moreover, in these two months, not only has there been no rain, but the river tides have also fallen sharply. There is no mountain flood flowing down the inland rivers, and no river flow irrigating them. They are almost dry and the bottoms can be seen. Therefore, the small boats from Wuhu to Nanling, Dongba, Xuancheng, Langxi, and other places have all had their construction blocked and have suspended navigation. The result of the dry sky and dry land is an extremely arid climate. Dust fills the air, suffocating people and endangering the mosquitoes and flies, which are taking advantage of the situation to extend their lives and are active everywhere. As a result, plagues are rampant. Malignant malaria, dysentery, and throat and eye diseases are spreading rapidly. According to recent reliable statistics, more than 2,000 people have died from seasonal diseases in various counties. Patients from the countryside are constantly being carried into the city for medical treatment. Although the Central Health Administration has sent personnel with medicines to various places for assistance, the region is vast, and the rescue personnel are coming and going in a hurry, with little effect. The Lunar Double Ninth Festival has passed, and the sky is still clear for thousands of miles. It seems that there is no hope for widespread rain in the near future. The future of people's food and the fierce flames of the plague are truly worrying. (24th)

Songjiang: Farmers in Xidongjing Robbed 64

In the county's Second District, Xidongjing Township, Sixth Bao, Third Jia, farmer Zhang Guitang's son, Zhang Caisheng, has an average family situation. On the 23rd at around 10 p.m., more than ten robbers, each carrying pistols, wooden sticks, flashlights, and hemp ropes, suddenly appeared. They broke through the bamboo wall and entered, opening the door to let the remaining robbers in. The victims were already fast asleep. They went straight into the bedroom, scaring the victims and preventing them from making any noise, and locked them in a room to ransack the place. After about an hour, they escaped with the stolen goods. After checking the losses of clothing and other items, the incident was reported to the Public Security Fifth Precinct for investigation.

Suzhou: Another Suspected Traitor Arrested 65

The Public Security Bureau here has arrested many suspected traitors disguised as beggars in recent days and detained them for investigation. Yesterday, a suspected traitor named Wang Huainan was arrested on a road outside the Panmen Japanese Concession. Director Zhang has ordered strict suppression of the general public who spread rumors to confuse people because the current situation is tense.

Collection of Land Tax Starts Successively 66

The county government has already started collecting the first installment of land tax. The second installment is now scheduled to start on December 1st. However, the general reduction of color has been submitted to the provincial government for approval. As for the rent collection issue, it has been decided to open the granaries on November 11th, with a general reduction of 15% in color. The discounted price has not yet been determined and will be based on recent rice prices.

Large Batch of Public Prostitute Licenses Revoked 67

Public prostitution in Suzhou has been open for a year. Due to the current situation, the business of public prostitutes at all levels is not thriving. Most of the first-class prostitutes have returned to other cities to work. Second and third-class prostitutes can barely maintain their business. The Prostitute Inspection Office of the Public Security Bureau has found that most of the second-class prostitutes are infected with diseases. Therefore, on the 25th, it was announced that the licenses of thirty-three second-class prostitutes and fifteen third-class prostitutes would be revoked, and they would not be allowed to receive customers. However, in recent days, private prostitutes have filled the inns inside and outside the city, and the authorities have strictly prohibited them.

Changshu: Strange Warship off Hupukou 68

At around 2 p.m. on the 24th, a strange warship suddenly appeared about two kilometers off Hupukou. The flags were unclear. After residents reported it, the Yuxun warship stationed in Hupuzhen observed it with a telescope. The warship had no flags, but it had anti-aircraft guns and wireless radio equipment. It also used small boats to patrol nearby. Its actions seemed to be measuring the water level. It left at around 5 p.m. The commander of the Zhenxun warship immediately reported to the county government by telephone. According to the observation of the villagers, there were symbols similar to Chinese phonetic alphabet characters on the stern of the warship, and it was undoubtedly a warship from a certain country.

Wuxi: Dispute over Loading and Unloading at Warehouses 69

In order to facilitate the transportation of goods, Shenxin Third Factory in this city specifically signed a cooperation agreement with the Lianglu Bureau to rent a place called Yangqi in the west of the city's train station to build a new Rentui warehouse. The project has been completed, and Ding Ruixian, a local resident, has been hired as the foreman to be responsible for all the loading and unloading matters of the factory. However, the Hubei gang of loading and unloading workers in the miscellaneous grain class of the train station, including Chen Renrui, Jin Decai, and Duan Tinghua, believed that the area was their business scope and opposed it as a group, demanding that they be responsible for the loading and unloading. Rong Desheng, the owner of the warehouse, believed that the warehouse was officially rented from the Road Bureau, and he should have the right to make his own decisions on all loading and unloading matters. Furthermore, the Fuxin warehouse in Shanghai and other warehouses have precedents to follow and are not bound by customs. Therefore, he rejected the unreasonable demands. Afterwards, the Hubei gang workers repeatedly stirred up trouble and instigated all the workers to sign a consultation agreement, stipulating four conditions: 1. They pledged to fight to the death for this matter. If a fight occurs, they will jointly be responsible for all litigation matters. 2. If they become disabled due to the fight, they will share 300 yuan in legal tender. 3. If they die in a fight, they will jointly contribute 600 yuan in legal tender. 4. Those who do not participate in the fight will be jointly driven out. Ding Ruixian discovered the consultation agreement and submitted it separately to the Public Security Bureau, the county government, and the Second District Commissioner's Office, requesting assistance and requesting prompt prohibition to avoid danger. Yesterday was the day the warehouse was scheduled to start work, and the workers were supposed to officially start work. However, about 200 Hubei gang workers went to cause trouble again,抢抢 (unable to translate), and seized the work. The police from the Sixth Precinct of the Public Security Bureau were dispatched to stop them, but it was ineffective. They had to let them do as they pleased. At the same time, the warehouse reported the situation to the county bureau, requesting action. The matter is currently under consideration, and it is unknown how it will be resolved.

Land Registration Proceeding Smoothly 70

The Land Administration Bureau of this county has a total land area of ​​1,928,620 mu. Since the preparation for land registration, the process has been going very smoothly. The entire third district has been completed in the area where registration is being carried out, and the bureau has issued land ownership certificates. The four districts, four, five, six, and seven, can also be completed around the beginning of the next month. The total area accounts for about half of the county. The remaining five districts, one, two, eight, nine, and ten, will begin registration around the middle of the next month. After the local court of this city was ordered to stop real estate registration, it was all handled by the Land Administration Bureau.

Danyang: Plague Epidemic in the Four Townships 71

Recently, there has been no rain for a long time, and the weather is extremely dry. Not only is farming difficult, but the malignant malaria in the four townships has also turned fierce again. In addition, dust and sand are flying, entering people's throats and noses. It is feared that throat diseases are likely to occur. In view of this, the county government has specially sent doctors with medicines to go to the villages in turns for diagnosis and treatment to avoid the spread.

Yangzhou: Guidance Committee Surveys the River Channel to the Yangtze River 72

The Guidance Committee of Huai River takes the project of channeling the river to the Yangtze River as urgent and needs to start the measurement first for the sake of design. It has appointed Shen Guanke as the captain of the measurement team to the Yangtze River and ordered him to take the staff to Jiangdu along the river for measurement. It is heard that the county government of the counties to the north of the Yangtze River have received the instructions from the Committee to assist and protect when the team arrives, and they have ordered the construction and public security bureaus and relevant district offices to follow the instructions.

Difficult Navigation in the Shallow Sections of the Canal 73

Since autumn, there has been very little rainfall in the area north of the Yangtze River, resulting in the failure to sow wheat until now. The water in the canal has dried up like in the cold winter. Places such as Malanwan and Baotawan are difficult to navigate. In terms of human affairs, due to the extreme autumn dryness, seasonal epidemics are prevalent, and the situation is very worrying.

Nantong: Signs of Drought Seen in Nantong Prefecture 74

It has been more than two months since the counties in Nantong Prefecture north of the Yangtze River have had any rainfall. The river water is shallow and dried up, and the soil is cracked. Vegetable prices have soared. The Frost's Descent solar term is approaching, and farmers are hoping for rain to sow wheat. Due to the disharmony of the climate, seasonal epidemics are very prevalent. At present, drought conditions have formed in urban and rural areas.

Unified Management of Flower Firms in Northern Jiangsu 75

The Jiangsu Provincial Cotton Production Improvement Office will start with the cotton-producing areas in northern Jiangsu, completing the registration of flower firms, implementing unified management, and eliminating inferior varieties and degenerated foreign cotton seeds. The provincial government has allocated 100,000 yuan for the cotton industry improvement fee and will not collect it from flower merchants.

Jiaxing: Drought Affects Agricultural Production 76

Since the beginning of autumn, there has been no rain in Jiaxing for a long time. The river water has dried up, and the soil has cracked. Although the late rice has already formed grains, due to the dryness, there will be many white ears. Rural crops, such as soybeans and vegetables, have mostly withered as a result. Broad beans and wheat cannot be sown. It is expected that the spring harvest next year will be greatly reduced.

Investigation and Prohibition of Private Collection of Grain Payments 77

The county government has reformed the collection system this time, setting up land registrars in various townships to be responsible for urging the payment of land tax. All former tax collectors and village scribes have been abolished, and the practice of drafting tax collection forms and going to the countryside to collect taxes has been stopped. Now, in order to eliminate abuses, the county government is deeply afraid that the dismissed tax collectors and village scribes will spread rumors and disrupt the situation in the countryside, and will fraudulently collect grain payments and extort fees in the name of the government. Yesterday, the county government specially ordered the township chiefs to pay attention to this at all times. If found, they should report to the police, arrest them, and send them to the county for legal action. In addition, in order to rectify land tax, the county government has ordered that foreign vegetable farmers who owe land tax should be required by the land registrars to have their tenants deduct rent to pay off the grain tax. Large households who owe land tax should also be handled in the same way.

Representatives from All Walks of Life and Relatives and Friends of Mr. Hu Offered Public Sacrifices to Chairman Hu Yesterday; Mayor Wu and Ye Gongchuo Served as Chief Sacrificers; the Entire City Lowered Flags and Suspended Entertainment to Express Condolences 78

Yesterday was the date of the national funeral of the late Mr. Hu Zhantang, Chairman of the Central Standing Committee. Representatives from all walks of life in this city held a public memorial service at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce at Tianhougong Bridge at 9 a.m. yesterday. More than 1,000 representatives from all walks of life extended the service until 3 p.m. Mayor Wu (Yu Hongjun acting) served as the chief sacrificer, and Tong Hangbai and Tao Baichuan served as assistant sacrificers. The entire city lowered flags and suspended entertainment for one day to express condolences. The relatives and friends of Mr. Hu recited scriptures and offered sacrifices at the Guoren Temple on Avenue du Lieutenant Colonel Moll in the French Concession. The details of each event are recorded below.

The Venue Arrangement was Solemn and Respectful

The venue for the public memorial service for the late Chairman Hu of the Central Standing Committee was set up in the grand auditorium of the Cloth Merchants Association at Tianhougong Bridge. A plain-colored archway and crossed party and national flags were set up at the main entrance, and a white cloth banner was hung with the words "Shanghai Municipal Representatives from All Walks of Life Hold a National Funeral Public Memorial Ceremony for the Late Chairman Hu." The flagpoles at the main entrance were lowered. The altar at the venue was also decorated with a plain-colored archway, with a portrait of the President and a portrait of the late Chairman Hu in the middle. The party and national flags were crossed on both sides, and the surroundings were filled with plain colors and wreaths sent by various circles. The front of the display stand was extremely solemn and respectful.

More Than 1,000 Representatives Attended

Yesterday, the representatives from all walks of life who participated in the public memorial service included Mayor Wu's representative Yu Hongjun, Tong Hangbai and Tao Baichuan from the Municipal Party Department, and all the staff, Pan Gongzhan from the Social Affairs Bureau, and the chiefs of various sections, Gan Xiaolai from the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, Fan Wei from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Wu Yihong from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Jiang Huaisu from the Municipal Defense Committee, Hu Tianseng and Shen Liangzhong from the New Life Movement Promotion Association, Tan Wenqing from the Public Works Bureau, Ma Youcheng from the Land Bureau, Li Dachao from the Aviation Association, Li Zhaohuan from the University Federation, Yu Zhenhui from the Municipal Farmers Association, Chen Guangfu and Lin Kanghou from the Banking Association, Lin Kecong from the Municipal Women's Association, Cao Zhigong from the First Special District Citizen's Association, Huang Xianggu from the French Concession Taxpayers' Association, Mao Yun from the Second Special District Citizen's Association, Shao Yanshan from the Money Exchange Association, Zhao Shusheng from the National Postal Workers' Union, Du Mengsen from the Cooperative Undertakings Promotion Association, Zhang Huiliang, Minister to Cuba, He Yuanming from the Accountants Association, and representatives from all levels of the Party Department, Doumi, Jewelry, Shipping, Sand and Gravel, Instruments and Stationery, Antiques, Silk and Satin, Candle Industry, Egg Factory, Knitting, Porcelain, and other trade associations, cigarette, hotel, military uniform, pharmaceutical, match, electrical machinery, rickshaw pullers, and other labor unions, as well as Ningbo, Nantong, and other fellow villagers associations, and representatives from Jinan, Men and Women's Public, Youth, and East China schools. From 9 a.m. to 3 p.m., more than 1,000 representatives attended.

Public Memorial Service by Representatives from All Walks of Life

At 9 a.m., the official public memorial service began. The Municipal Public Security Bureau Band played mournful music. Mayor Wu's representative Yu Hongjun served as the chief sacrificer, and Tong Hangbai and Tao Baichuan from the Municipal Party Department served as assistant sacrificers. Wang Manyun read the memorial text, and Zhang Hanyun and Ren Bin served as the masters of ceremonies. The ceremony was as follows: (1) All stand in silence. (2) Play mournful music. (3) The chief sacrificer takes his place. (4) The assistant sacrificers take their places. (5) Sing the Party song. (6) Bow three times to the Party and National flags, the President's portrait, and the portrait of the late Chairman Hu. (7) Remain silent for three minutes. (8) Offer flowers. (9) Read the memorial text. (The memorial text was recorded in yesterday's newspaper, omitted). (11) Play mournful music. (12) The ceremony is completed.

Public Memorial Text of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations and employees of the Chamber of Commerce also held a memorial service. Wang Xiaolai served as the chief sacrificer. The memorial text reads: "Six months after the passing of Mr. Hu Zhantang, Chairman of the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee, the nation remembers the elders and holds a national funeral ceremony in Guangzhou. Today, government officials, people, and organizations in various places also perform the ceremony of public memorial service to express their condolences. Therefore, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations follow the example of various organizations and respectfully send representatives to offer sacrifices and connect them with the text: Since you returned to the West, the sea has changed several times. Unsubmissive, troops are stationed on the outskirts. In the city of Five Rams, the wind and cranes spread throughout, and the generals are tired of war. Returning the banners to the front line is for the benefit of the country. The South's gold and the East's arrows clear the eight sides and the sea is safe. Relying on your legacy, we reform and face. The spirit-like style relies on, and is drawn into joy. In the month of Xiaochun, the wind is harmonious and the sun is bright, and the pines and cypresses are lush. The beautiful city is forever fixed, and the Yunshan of Xianshou is forever loved by all. How to admire and repay, the Pingfan is recommended."

Relatives and Friends of Mr. Hu Held a Separate Memorial Service

Yesterday, in addition to the public memorial service held by various circles at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the relatives, friends, and former colleagues of Mr. Hu in Shanghai, including Ye Gongchuo, He Shizhen, Wei Daoming, He Shimei, Zhang Dingfan, Zhou Yongneng, Xue Dubi, Hu Puan, Sun Jinya, Yang Shukan, Chen Qun, Yang Hu, Xiao Jinfang, Xu Chongzhi, and the Buddhist Association Yuanying, initiated the recitation of scriptures at Guoren Temple on Avenue du Lieutenant Colonel Moll in the French Concession and held a public memorial service at 10 a.m. Those who attended included Ye Gongchuo, He Shizhen, Wei Daoming, He Shimei, Wang Zhinan, Zhang Zhiben, Zhang Dingfan, Zhou Yongneng, Xue Dubi, Hu Zongduo, Hu Puan, Sun Jinya, Yang Shukan, Chen Qun, Yang Hu, Xiao Jinfang, Xu Chongzhi, Li Dachao, and the Buddhist Association Yuanying, totaling more than 400 people. Ye Gongchuo served as the chief sacrificer, Zhou Bogan served as the master of ceremonies, and Luo Gusun read the memorial text. The memorial text is recorded as follows: "On October 25th, the 25th year of the Republic of China, on the date of the national funeral of Mr. Hu Zhantang, Chairman of the Central Standing Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang, old friends in Shanghai respectfully offer seasonal delicacies and thin wine, as well as flowers and fruits, to the spirit of Mr. Hu and bid farewell, saying: Alas, Mr. Your aspirations were not fully expressed, and tears fell first. Considering the sorrowful feelings, the peak of the mountain and the riverside cannot be reached. How can great virtue reach this? Through the construction of extraordinary talent, the safety of the universe is straightened. The President is like Yan Zeng, and is truly a teacher for the whole country. It is hoped that the raging waves will be turned back, and the precarious building can be supported. The poor people are placed in a comfortable environment, and the dying sores are raised. He declares great justice for our party, and makes great harmony the basis. It is hoped that the mountains and rivers inside and outside will be unharmed. What's more, the dangers and obstacles have been fully tasted. How can we expect the inexhaustible poetry to exist, and the posthumous works to enjoy the eternal broom? From then on, there will be endless regrets and sorrows, and we will watch a game of chess in grief. Alas, the bright soul will not be worn away, the iron liver will not be cold, the old generation will be carved away, and the legacy is still new. The essence is one, the holy is the spirit, accumulating morality can be literature, and the universe admires the former. He wields a spear to defend the country and wishes that strong men will rise again in the world. Alas, alas, enjoy!"

Sun Jingya's memorial text reads: "On October 25th, the 25th year of the Republic of China, on the date of holding a national funeral for Mr. Hu Zhantang in Guangzhou, Sun Jingya, a comrade living in Shanghai, respectfully offers flowers to the spirit of Mr. Hu and writes the words: Alas, after the President's death, looking around at his comrades, who can succeed in continuing his work and legacy better than you? His talent and wisdom are outstanding, and his reputation has spread since he was a weak youth. His character is upright, and even his mentors and guardians are not as good as him. His achievements are outstanding, and they are inscribed on tripods and utensils. His knowledge is vast, and he combines Chinese and foreign into one. He distinguishes between right and wrong, truth and falsehood, and speaks clearly and does not hesitate. Those secular so-called interests, gains and losses, praise and slander, misfortune and blessing, you disdained to avoid them. He was always calm and composed, and he took on the rugged road of the world, casting the principles as laws, and hoped to have an end from the beginning. How can we plan for the end of the war, and feel the red fox and black crow? From then on, he recuperated in Xiangjiang, until he changed his mind in Guangzhou. What caused you anxiety was that all the facilities did not conform to the President's legacy. When the entire Party did not forget the old veterans, and unanimously pushed the central hub, the people depended on it, and relied on this person to drive him. You returned from overseas, and the situation was the same. You felt that the square and the round were chiseled, and it was still inevitable to disagree. Nai Zhi Luofu, Douyun spit beads, his mouth did not stop chanting, and his hands did not stop writing, regretting the setting sun's wings, and scratching his head with hesitation. In your life, you have heard of the present, and your death has been passed on to future generations. It is enough to believe that my way is not alone, and when the bad news arrives, the apes cry and the cranes scream, the sea roars and the rocks call, the grass and trees contain tears, the fish and insects are wet, the friendly countries are shocked and grieved, and the mourners are full of roads. The whole country is in a panic, like a leaking boat meeting the wind and rain, and it is unbearable to cry and sob. What's more, in the past, we followed you, showed each other our hearts, and imprinted our dreams together. When Jiacheng is forever strong, we are ashamed to hold the hands of you. In the face of the wind, we cry for both public and private, and we miss you, the love and sincerity of our comrades, which cannot be seen again, and the national crisis is getting worse day by day, and it is dangerous to be scattered."

Lowering Flags and Suspending Entertainment to Express Condolences

Yesterday, because it was the date of the national funeral ceremony for the late Chairman Hu, in addition to the public memorial service held by the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Government at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, and the relatives, friends, and former colleagues of Mr. Hu in Shanghai who set up a separate memorial service at Guoren Temple, the Party and government agencies announced that the flags would be lowered for one day in the city, and entertainment would be suspended to express condolences. All the amusement parks, cinemas, theaters, and radio stations in the Chinese community were closed yesterday to commemorate him. In addition, in order to commemorate Mr. Hu's national funeral, the central government ordered the Postal Service Administration to order the post offices in various places to add a long square commemorative postmark of 18 characters on the letters that passed yesterday, which read "Inherit the legacy of the late Chairman Hu and complete the National Revolution of the Three Principles of the People."

Shenxin No. 2 Factory is Ready; Worker Registration Begins Today; Officially Starts Work on the 29th 80

Chairman Ma Lin of Qinghai Province Will Go to Mecca Tomorrow; Forming a Chinese Muslim Pilgrimage Group; A Total of More Than 130 People 82

According to the New Life News Agency, after Qinghai Provincial Government Chairman Ma Lin went to Beijing to meet President Chiang and other authorities, he borrowed the residence of Zhu Shaoliang, director of the Gansu-Qinghai Border Pacification Office, on Avenue Massenet, and continued to seek medical treatment for his epilepsy. Yesterday, it was learned that Mr. Ma and his son Bu Yuan, as well as Ah Heng (i.e. religious teacher) Ma Zhengqing, Ma Li, and attendants, gathered Muslims from the northwest provinces of Qinghai, Ningxia, and Gansu, Ma Qishan, commander of the Fifteenth Route Army, and others to form a Chinese Muslim pilgrimage group to Mecca, totaling more than 130 people (including six women). They are scheduled to depart tomorrow on the Blue Funnel Line's Asohalion, heading for Mecca (Kingdom of Hejaz). All the departure procedures have been completed by Mr. Jin Ziyun of the Xiaotaoyuan Mosque in Laoximen. The meals along the way will be provided on board, and the Muslims will cook their own meals. Mr. Ma and others are scheduled to board the ship at Xinguang Pier tomorrow morning. Mayor Wu Tiecheng of this city, Yang Hu, commander of the Songhu Garrison, and other groups such as the mosques in this city and the Humanitarian Monthly Society will send representatives to the ship to welcome them. The group's planned itinerary is as follows: Shanghai to Hong Kong in two days, stop for one day, Hong Kong to Singapore in five days, stop for two days, and then change ships directly to Jeddah, passing through Penang, Colombo, and Aden, to land at the port of Jeddah. The journey from Jeddah to Mecca is all desert and requires riding camels, which takes about two days to reach Mecca. The entire journey takes 27 days. According to the Muslim belief that going to the Kaaba (i.e. the Muslim holy land) is one of the five pillars of Islam (i.e. Shahada, Salat, Zakat, Sawm, and Hajj), all Muslims should visit the Kaaba in Mecca once in their lifetime.

Dasheng Cotton Mill Preparing to Resume Operations 84

According to Shen Shi News Agency, Dasheng Cotton Mill No. 1, which suspended operations last year, has recently been preparing to resume operations due to the increase in purchasing power in China's rural areas and the skyrocketing sales of cotton yarn and cloth, resulting in a shortage of supply and a return to the golden age of the European War. The Ten-End-of-Month Period is Approaching; Yesterday, Money Dealers Discussed the Internal Market Rate; Interest Rate of 5.5 Yuan per Thousand Yuan for Six Months; About 100 Million Yuan in Loans from Shanghai, Ningbo, and Hankou are Due; The Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications Handle Interbank Lending as Usual 85

The credit loans of Shanghai money dealers at the end of October are approaching their due date. The Money Dealers Association held a meeting yesterday to discuss the internal market rate. Representatives from various Ningbo and Hankou dealers who have extended loans in Shanghai were sent to Shanghai. The Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications handled interbank lending as usual. The details are as follows:

Shanghai and Ningbo Dealers All Accommodating

As the end of October approaches, various money dealers have already contacted the industrial and commercial firms that have borrowed money to negotiate long-term credit loans. For those with a good credit history, the terms are extended to the end of April next year. The collection and settlement of both silver and money businesses have become busy. Money dealers in Ningbo, Ruichang, Shenkang, Dunyu, Yikang, etc., all have long-term credit loans in Shanghai, either extending them on their own or entrusting them to colleagues and affiliates. They have now successively sent representatives to Shanghai to negotiate. At the same time, money dealers in Hankou who have extended loans in Shanghai have also sent representatives to Shanghai to negotiate. The above-mentioned Ningbo and Hankou dealers will also follow the Shanghai money dealers' approach to Shanghai credit loans, and those with good credit will be accommodated with term extensions.

Money Dealers Meeting Internal Market Rate

The Money Dealers Association held a meeting of managers of various member dealers at the Ningbo Road Clubhouse at 1:00 PM yesterday to discuss the internal market rate. More than 40 managers, including those from Fuyuan, Zifeng, Fukang, Dade, Zhiyu, Tongrun, Tongyu, Zhentai, Huifeng, Gengyu, Qingcheng, Hongsheng, Shenyuan, Chengyu, Shunkang, Yuansheng, Cunde, Yida, Hengxun, etc., attended, including Pei Yunqing, Shao Yanshan, Liu Wuqiao, Qian Yuansheng, Xu Jingxiang, Zai Jiemei, Zhao Songyuan, Xi Jiming, Zhang Dafu, and others. Shao Yanshan presided over the meeting. After exchanging opinions on the ten-end-of-month long-term credit loan period, the discussion began, and it was decided that the "internal rate" would be 5.5 yuan. The meeting adjourned at 2:00 PM.

Various Dealers Begin Settling Internal Accounts

A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency learned from money dealers yesterday that the internal rate refers to the interest rate on long-term credit deposits of money dealers with their shareholders or colleagues. For example, 5.5 yuan means that the interest for six months on every 1,000 yuan of national currency is 5.5 yuan, which is equivalent to an annual interest rate of 1.1%. Starting from today, all dealers will settle interest on long-term credit deposits of shareholders in accordance with the internal market rate. In addition, the total amount of long-term credit loans due at the end of October from 49 Shanghai remittance money dealers is approximately 70 million yuan. The total amount from Ningbo dealers is approximately 20 million yuan, and the total amount from Hankou and other places is approximately 10 million yuan. The total of the above is approximately 100 million yuan.

Three Banks Handle Interbank Lending

In order to adjust interbank finance, the Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications previously organized a lending committee. The fund was guaranteed by the three banks in a 4:4:2 ratio. When colleagues needed it, they could apply to the three banks for borrowing with deeds, goods, etc. The interest rate was particularly low. In view of the approaching end of October this year, it was decided to handle interbank lending as in previous years. In addition, of the 18 million yuan that the money dealers borrowed from the three banks during the Dragon Boat Festival last year, 10 million yuan has not yet been repaid. This year, the dealers at the end of October do not need to borrow from the three banks again in fact because the market has become active.

He Huaide's Comfortable Flight Across the Pacific; The Future Progress of Aviation is Unlimited 86

The Zi Lin News reported that Mr. He Huaide, General Manager and Editor-in-Chief of the New York World, arrived in Shanghai on Saturday afternoon on a trans-Pacific commercial plane. After getting off the plane, he told guests: "This flight was not as tense as you might imagine. Of all the trips from the United States to Shanghai, this was the fastest." He stated that on Monday, October 12, at 5:10 PM, he boarded a full-night sleeper plane in New York, crossed the United States, and landed in San Francisco at 11:00 AM the next morning. The Philippine Clipper flying boat departed from Alameda on Wednesday (October 14) afternoon and arrived in Honolulu at 7:00 AM the next morning. On Friday (October 16), it continued to advance to Manila and landed in the Philippines on Tuesday, October 20. It flew out of Manila on the 23rd and arrived in Macau and Hong Kong the next day. The residents of Macau welcomed it very much, while Hong Kong was not as enthusiastic as Macau. The merits of the Philippine Clipper cannot be exhausted in a few words. The decoration of the boat is very gorgeous, with three large rooms, one of which is a lounge for passengers to use. Sitting in it, one feels quite comfortable, so guests often gather here to play cards, dice, chat, or read books, according to their wishes. There is another room with four couches for guests who feel slightly tired from the fast trip. He only spent one night on the flying boat during the entire journey from Alameda to Honolulu and felt very comfortable. The two places are 2,400 miles apart, and it took 17 hours to complete the journey. Among the places stopped on the way from Honolulu to Manila, Guam is a giant island with excellent scenery, and Wake and Midway are both small islands. Looking down from an altitude of 10,000 feet, they seem even smaller. However, all the islands are equipped with new and beautiful hotels, with complete sanitary facilities and delicious meals, and fishing on the beach is especially enjoyable. Two years ago, Mr. He accompanied Mr. Clipper of Pan American Airlines on a trip to South America on the Brazilian Clipper. Since then, he has repeatedly discussed with Mr. Clipper the possibility of direct flights to China, but he never expected to be able to make this trip from New York. Mr. He said that the current Clipper is like comparing a rickshaw to a car compared to the original Clipper. The current one weighs 52,000 pounds and carries 24 passengers. A new flying boat weighing 82,000 pounds is currently under construction and will be able to carry 40 passengers. This flight is enough to prove the great progress of aviation, and the progress in the future is still limitless. He encountered various climates along the way, and even encountered storms, but being in the boat, he did not feel it. None of the guests experienced "airsickness," and the comfort was no less than that of a ship crossing the Pacific Ocean. Mr. Clipper also said that he was extremely satisfied with this trip. Pan American Airlines regards the Pacific business as the most important of all the routes operated by the company. This visit to China is to pay tribute to the company's representatives in China and various government officials. The cooperation given by the Chinese government is extremely grateful. Mr. Clipper will stay in China for a long time, and after visiting Nanjing and North China, he will return to the United States via Europe.

Six Companies Decide to Increase Yangtze River Shallow Water Fees Again, Effective November 1 88

The six companies, including the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the privately-owned Sanbei Company, Ning Shao Company, the British-owned Taikoo Company, Jardine Matheson Company, and the Japanese-owned Nisshin Kisen Kaisha, decided, in view of the shallow water of the Yangtze River and the slower navigation, to increase the shallow water fee for goods starting from October 19. The Merger of Zhonghui Bank and Jiangzhe Bank; The Inaugural Meeting of the Merger was Held Yesterday; The Total Capital is 3.5 Million Yuan in National Currency; Du Yuesheng, Chen Guangfu, and Others were Elected as Directors and Supervisors; It was Decided that Zhonghui would be the Head Office and Jiangzhe would be Changed to a Branch Office 89

Zhonghui Bank and Jiangzhe Bank, two major banks in this city with huge amounts of capital, implemented a merger to increase their strength and expand their business, creating a new era in China's banking industry. The two banks held a shareholders' meeting to establish the merger on the second floor of Zhonghui Bank at 3:00 PM yesterday. The articles of association were amended, the total capital was 3.5 million yuan, 15 directors and 5 supervisors were elected, and it was decided that the merger would be implemented on November 2. A reporter from Xin Xin News Agency recorded the details as follows:

Shareholders' Meeting

The inaugural meeting of the merger was held yesterday, with a total of 24,300 shares and 126 households, or 20,516 rights, represented by the two banks, exceeding the legal quorum. Chairman Du Yuesheng was publicly elected to preside over the meeting. He reported on the merger procedures and the process, and said that the three-month period for public announcement by the two banks in accordance with the law was about to expire, so today's shareholders' meeting was convened to establish the merger, amend the articles of association, elect directors and supervisors, and discuss all matters. Next, the articles of association were amended and it was resolved that: (1) The total capital is 3.5 million yuan in national currency; (2) The number of directors is increased to 15 and the number of supervisors is increased to 5; (3) The merger will be implemented from November 2; (4) After the merger, the Zhonghui Bank on Aiduya Road will be called the head office, and the original site of Jiangzhe Bank on Jiangxi Road will be changed to a branch office of Zhonghui Bank and continue to operate. After the discussion, the directors and supervisors were elected, and the meeting adjourned at about 5:00 PM.

Elected Directors and Supervisors

The election results were announced, and the elected directors were Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Chen Guangfu, Ye Zhuotang, Tang Shoumin, Wu Yunzhai, Wu Qiding, Zhou Wenrui, Zhu Rushan, Zhang Weirou, Liu Jisheng, Zhu Yicai, Jin Tingsun, Zhang Fayao, Wu Ruiyuan, etc., totaling 15 people. The alternate directors were Xu Maochang and Bei Runsheng. The elected supervisors were Jiang Yiping, Wang Zhongqi, Ding Mengxing, Zhang Jiguang, Zhang Qiyang, etc., totaling 5 people. The alternate supervisors were Lin Lanpu and Xu Boxiong.

Board Meeting

A reporter from Xin Xin News Agency learned that the elected directors will hold their first board meeting within days to elect the chairman and managing directors. It was also learned that the deposits and loans of the two banks have increased during the preparation for the merger, which has been well received by the domestic economic and financial circles. Now that the merger is about to be implemented, and giants in the banking industry such as Chen Guangfu, Tang Shoumin, and Ye Zhuotang have been elected as directors, the strength will be even more solid. The expansion and development of future operations can be assured.
